##### **Optimizing Abstractive Summarization With Fine-Tuned PEGASUS**
2606.25462v1 by Sadiul Arefin Rafi, Naimur Rahman, Kazi Nazibul Islam, Ha-mim Ahmad, Farig Yousuf Sadeque

Abstractive text summarization is the technique of generating a short and concise summary comprising the salient ideas of a source text without making a subset of the salient sentences from the source text. The introduction of transformer models such as BART, T5, and PEGASUS has made this sort of summarization process more efficient and accurate. The objective of this paper is to fine-tune PEGASUS on the XL-Sum English corpus to achieve a better performance compared to the baseline mT5 model. The performance of the generated summaries from the fine-tuned model is evaluated using the ROUGE metric, which basically compares the auto-generated summaries with human-created summaries. To the best of our knowledge, the results from our fine-tuned PEGASUS model give a state-of-the-art performance on the XL-Sum English Corpus. 摘要：抽象文本摘要是生成一個簡短且精煉的摘要的技術，該摘要包含來源文本的主要思想，而不是從來源文本中提取出一部分突出的句子。像 BART、T5 和 PEGASUS 等Transformer模型的引入使這種摘要過程變得更加高效和準確。本文的目標是對 XL-Sum 英文語料庫上的 PEGASUS 進行微調，以達到比基線 mT5 模型更好的性能。從微調模型生成的摘要的性能是使用 ROUGE 指標進行評估的，該指標基本上是將自動生成的摘要與人類創建的摘要進行比較。據我們所知，我們微調的 PEGASUS 模型在 XL-Sum 英文語料庫上達到了最先進的性能。為了量化改進，ROUGE-1 分數提高了 4.04%，ROUGE-2 分數增加了 15.25%，ROUGE-L 分數從基線模型提高了 3.39%。

##### **Learning with a Single Rollout via Monte Carlo Pass@k Critic**
2606.25451v1 by Fengdi Che, Yang Liu, Lei Yu, Meng Cao, Tong Che, Rupam Mahmood, Dale Schuurmans

Estimating token-level advantages in reinforcement learning (RL) for language models remains challenging because scaling up episodic experience collection is expensive. The difficulty intensifies for baseline advantage estimation methods, where repeated sampling causes trajectories to diverge into substantially different reasoning prefixes. In this context, RL algorithms such as GRPO prove limited: an outcome reward is too sparse to be attributed to specific actions like intermediate steps, and comparisons across sampled traces are non-trivial because they are heterogeneous. To mitigate both the computational cost of repeated sampling and the difficulty of credit assignment, we study single-rollout proximal policy optimization (SR-PPO) featuring token-level credit assignment in RL for language models. Instead of estimating advantages by normalizing episodic returns within the candidate group, we train a calibrated token-level credit critic using Monte Carlo outcomes from one rollout per prompt. Specifically, we use the critic to predict the Pass@k success probability at the prompt prefix, which is derived from a Pass@1 attempt. This choice yields a more selective learning signal than Pass@1: it discounts easily solved prefixes while prioritizing hard ones whose success probability remains marginal. We show that as $k$ increases, Pass@k converges to a reachability indicator, reflecting whether a prefix can lead to at least one successful continuation. In an explicit state graph, the limit ($k \rightarrow \infty$) can be computed in $O(|V|+|E|)$ time, offering a promising surrogate for direct credit assignment without the need to sample contrastive traces. As an initial validation, SR-PPO exhibits stable learning dynamics, along with consistent gains in Pass@128 success rates on mathematical reasoning benchmarks such as HMMT26 and AIME24.

摘要：估算語言模型中強化學習（RL）的標記級優勢仍然具有挑戰性，因為擴大情節經驗收集的成本昂貴。對於基準優勢估計方法，這一困難加劇，因為重複取樣會導致軌跡分歧成為實質上不同的推理前綴。在這種情況下，像 GRPO 這樣的 RL 算法顯得有限：結果獎勵過於稀疏，無法歸因於特定行動，例如中間步驟，而跨取樣痕跡的比較則因其異質性而變得不平凡。為了減輕重複取樣的計算成本和信用分配的困難，我們研究了單次回合的近端策略優化（SR-PPO），該方法在語言模型中具有標記級的信用分配。我們不通過在候選組內正規化情節回報來估算優勢，而是使用每個提示的一次回合的蒙特卡洛結果訓練一個經過校準的標記級信用評估器。具體而言，我們使用該評估器來預測提示前綴的 Pass@k 成功概率，這是從 Pass@1 嘗試中得出的。這一選擇產生了比 Pass@1 更具選擇性的學習信號：它對容易解決的前綴進行折扣，同時優先考慮那些成功概率仍然邊際的困難前綴。我們顯示，隨著 $k$ 的增加，Pass@k 收斂到一個可達性指標，反映一個前綴是否可以導致至少一次成功的延續。在顯式狀態圖中，極限（$k \rightarrow \infty$）可以在 $O(|V|+|E|)$ 時間內計算，提供了一個有前景的替代方案，用於直接信用分配，而無需取樣對比痕跡。作為初步驗證，SR-PPO 展示了穩定的學習動態，以及在數學推理基準（如 HMMT26 和 AIME24）上的 Pass@128 成功率的一致增長。

##### **The Generalization Spectrum: A Chromatographic Approach to Evaluating Learning Algorithms**
2606.25450v2 by Jinghan Zhang, Zerui Cheng, Shiqi Chen, Ge Zhang, Wenhao Huang, Jiashuo Liu, Junxian He, Tianle Cai

Traditional evaluations measure a learning algorithm's final performance on an i.i.d. test set, reducing learning to a single aggregate score. This approach obscures a fundamental question: to what extent does learning from a specific example generalize to others? Such per-sample generalization, akin to learning by analogy in human cognition, captures how far the knowledge extracted from one example can transfer, yet remains invisible to standard benchmarks. We introduce the Generalization Spectrum, an evaluation framework designed to expose this hidden dimension. For each training example, we construct a controlled suite of test variants arranged by increasing transfer distance, from exact recall to implementation transfer across languages, context transfer under complete narrative re-framing, category-matched in-domain problems, and an unpaired baseline. By tracking performance across these distances, we reveal not just whether an algorithm learns, but how far that learning extends. We instantiate this framework on competitive programming, using a selection-and-synthesis pipeline seeded with recent problems to mitigate contamination. We first compare three canonical learning paradigms under matched memorization. RL converts memorization into near-transfer more efficiently than SFT-family baselines, while ICL exhibits strong but correspondence-dependent transfer. We then use the Spectrum to diagnose within-family variants. The resulting profiles show that local gains need not expand the generalization radius: abstractions and hints mainly lift local transfer, RFT preserves a stronger far-transfer tail than reference SFT, and self-distillation or hint-assisted RL can reduce far transfer even when local transfer or optimization improves.

摘要：傳統評估測量學習算法在獨立同分佈（i.i.d.）測試集上的最終表現，將學習簡化為單一的綜合分數。這種方法掩蓋了一個基本問題：從特定範例學習在多大程度上可以推廣到其他範例？這種逐樣本的推廣，類似於人類認知中的類比學習，捕捉了從一個範例中提取的知識可以轉移的遠度，但在標準基準中仍然是不可見的。我們引入了泛化光譜，一個旨在揭示這一隱藏維度的評估框架。對於每個訓練範例，我們構建了一套受控的測試變體，按轉移距離遞增排列，從精確回憶到跨語言的實施轉移、在完全敘事重構下的上下文轉移、類別匹配的內部問題，以及一個未配對的基準。通過追蹤這些距離上的表現，我們揭示的不僅是算法是否學習，而是該學習延伸的距離。我們在競爭性編程上實現了這一框架，使用一個由近期問題種子生成的選擇和綜合管道來減少污染。我們首先在匹配記憶下比較三種經典的學習範式。強化學習（RL）比SFT家族基準更有效地將記憶轉化為近轉移，而即時學習（ICL）則展現出強但依賴於對應的轉移。我們接著使用光譜來診斷家族內的變體。結果的輪廓顯示，局部增益不一定擴大泛化半徑：抽象和提示主要提升局部轉移，RFT保留比參考SFT更強的遠轉移尾部，而自我蒸餾或提示輔助的RL即使在局部轉移或優化改善的情況下，也可能減少遠轉移。

##### **LibEvoBench: Probing Temporal Knowledge Stratification in Code Generation Models**
2606.25402v1 by Daniele Cipollone, Sergey Titov, Maliheh Izadi, Egor Bogomolov, Arie van Deursen

Large software projects often depend on older versions of libraries, even as APIs continue to evolve across releases. This creates a challenge for LLMs: they must maintain knowledge of multiple API versions, not merely the latest or most common one. However, current LLMs are trained on temporally mixed corpora and lack explicit mechanisms for such version-specific reasoning, leading to anachronistic errors - calling APIs as they exist in a different library version. To systematically evaluate this phenomenon, we introduce LibEvoBench, a multi-task benchmark spanning multiple versions of widely used Python libraries, along with a new metric, the Software Evolution Understanding Score (SEUS), to measure models' consistency when working with evolving APIs. Our results show that state-of-the-art models are largely version-oblivious: performance degrades for evolving APIs, while for stable APIs it remains the same across versions. Moreover, simply specifying the target version provides no benefit, while relevant documentation significantly boosts models' accuracy. These findings highlight a systematic limitation of current training paradigms and motivate new approaches for temporally grounded knowledge in code generation.

摘要：大型軟體專案通常依賴於舊版本的函式庫，即使 API 在各個版本中持續演變。這對 LLMs 造成了一個挑戰：它們必須維持對多個 API 版本的知識，而不僅僅是最新或最常見的版本。然而，當前的 LLMs 在時間上混合的語料庫上進行訓練，缺乏針對這種版本特定推理的明確機制，導致了時代錯誤——以不同函式庫版本中的 API 方式進行調用。為了系統性地評估這一現象，我們引入了 LibEvoBench，一個跨越多個廣泛使用的 Python 函式庫版本的多任務基準，以及一個新的指標，軟體演進理解分數（SEUS），用於衡量模型在處理演變中的 API 時的一致性。我們的結果顯示，最先進的模型在很大程度上對版本無感：對於演變中的 API，性能下降，而對於穩定的 API，性能在各版本之間保持不變。此外，僅僅指定目標版本並沒有帶來任何好處，而相關文檔則顯著提高了模型的準確性。這些發現突顯了當前訓練範式的系統性限制，並激勵了對於在代碼生成中實現時間基礎知識的新方法。

##### **Offline Multi-agent Continual Cooperation via Skill Partition and Reuse**
2606.25389v1 by Yuchen Xiao, Lei Yuan, Ruiqi Xue, Tieyue Yin, Yang Yu

Extracting skills from multi-agent offline dataset improves learning efficiency via sharing task-invariant coordination skills among tasks. In settings where tasks occur sequentially and the space of skills grows exponentially, existing approaches that rely on heuristically designed and fixed-sized skill libraries struggle to resolve the problem of distributional shift and interference, facing catastrophic forgetting and plasticity loss. To address this problem and endow agents with the ability to continually discover and reuse coordination skills in open-environment, we propose COMAD, a principled framework for Continual Offline Multi-agent Skill Discovery via Skill Partition and Reuse. We first discover skills from mixed multi-agent behavior data with an auto-encoder to transform coordination knowledge into reusable coordination skills. Then we construct a skill-augmented policy learning objective with multi-head architectures, explicitly guiding the advantage function with reusable skills identified via a density-based reusability estimator. Theoretical analysis shows our method approximates the optimum of a continual skill discovery problem. Empirical results across diverse MARL benchmarks show that COMAD continually expands its skill library to mitigate interference, achieving superior forward and backward transfer for task streams compared to multiple baselines.

摘要：提取多智能體離線數據集中的技能透過在任務之間共享任務不變的協調技能來提高學習效率。 在任務按順序發生且技能空間指數增長的情況下，依賴於啟發式設計和固定大小技能庫的現有方法難以解決分佈轉移和干擾問題，面臨災難性遺忘和可塑性損失。 為了解決這個問題並賦予智能體在開放環境中持續發現和重用協調技能的能力，我們提出了COMAD，一個基於原則的持續離線多智能體技能發現框架，通過技能劃分和重用。 我們首先使用自編碼器從混合多智能體行為數據中發現技能，將協調知識轉化為可重用的協調技能。 然後，我們構建了一個技能增強的策略學習目標，使用多頭架構，明確指導優勢函數，並利用基於密度的可重用性估計器識別的可重用技能。 理論分析顯示我們的方法近似於持續技能發現問題的最優解。 在多樣的MARL基準測試中的實證結果顯示，COMAD持續擴展其技能庫以減輕干擾，實現了相較於多個基準的任務流的優越前向和後向轉移。

##### **TheoremGraph: Bridging Formal and Informal Mathematics**
2606.25363v1 by Simon Kurgan, Evan Wang, Eric Leonen, Sophie Szeto, Luke Alexander, Artemii Remizov, Jarod Alper, Giovanni Inchiostro, Vasily Ilin

Mathematical knowledge is organized around statements and their dependencies, but this structure is exposed unevenly: informal papers cite mostly at the document level, while formal libraries record fine-grained dependencies over a much smaller body of mathematics. We introduce TheoremGraph, a unified statement-level dependency graph spanning both informal and formal mathematics. On the informal side, we parse 11.7M theorem-like environments from mathematics arXiv and recover 18.3M candidate directed dependencies, each labeled by the extractor that proposed it so downstream users can trade coverage for precision. On the formal side, we release LeanGraph, a Lean 4 elaborator-level extractor producing 388,105 declaration nodes and 11.3M typed edges across 25 Lean projects. We bridge the two graphs by embedding generated natural-language slogans into a shared semantic space, linking related statements across papers and across the informal/formal divide; an LLM judge affirms 47,952 such matches above a 0.8 cosine floor, with the judge-acceptance rate rising from 48% across the floor to 87% in the >=0.9 tier. On formal concept retrieval, our name-and-signature representation with graph expansion comes within 0.5pp of LeanSearch v2's reranked Recall@10 (0.775 vs. 0.780) without an LM reranker. We release the dataset, extractors, HTTP API, and MCP interface as infrastructure for mathematical search, attribution, and retrieval-augmented reasoning, available at theoremsearch.com and huggingface.co/datasets/uw-math-ai/theorem-matching.

摘要：數學知識圍繞著陳述及其依賴關係組織，但這一結構的展現並不均衡：非正式論文主要在文檔層面引用，而正式庫則在更小的數學範疇內記錄細粒度的依賴關係。我們介紹了TheoremGraph，一個統一的陳述層級依賴圖，涵蓋了非正式和正式數學。在非正式方面，我們從數學arXiv中解析了11.7M類似定理的環境，並恢復了18.3M候選有向依賴，每個依賴都由提出者標記，以便下游用戶可以在覆蓋率和精確度之間進行取捨。在正式方面，我們釋出了LeanGraph，一個Lean 4展開器級別的提取器，產生了388,105個聲明節點和11.3M個類型邊，涵蓋25個Lean項目。我們通過將生成的自然語言口號嵌入共享語義空間來橋接這兩個圖，將相關陳述連結於論文之間以及非正式/正式的界限；一個LLM評判者確認了47,952個這樣的匹配，其餘的餘弦值在0.8以上，評判者接受率從地板的48%上升到>=0.9層的87%。在正式概念檢索方面，我們的名稱和簽名表示法與圖擴展的Recall@10在LeanSearch v2的重新排序結果中相差僅0.5個百分點（0.775對0.780），且未使用LM重新排序器。我們釋放了數據集、提取器、HTTP API和MCP介面，作為數學搜索、歸因和檢索增強推理的基礎設施，並可在theoremsearch.com和huggingface.co/datasets/uw-math-ai/theorem-matching獲得。

##### **Agentic Knowledge Tracing: A Multi-Agent LLM Architecture for Stealth Assessment of Financial Literacy in Serious Games**
2606.25358v1 by Gabriel Santos, Rita Julia, Marcelo Nascimento

Assessing financial literacy during gameplay without disrupting the learning experience remains a key challenge in serious games for education. We present the Agentic BKT pipeline, a multi-agent large language model architecture for stealth assessment of financial competencies from open-ended gameplay events. The pipeline processes events from a 2D platformer serious game aligned with the OECD/INFE financial literacy framework through four phases: (1) the game captures every player decision as a structured event log; (2) an LLM event classifier labels each action on a four-point rubric validated against three domain experts (Fleiss kappa = 0.624, substantial agreement); (3) four domain-specific agents specializing in risk mitigation, investing, spending, and credit management perform session-level reasoning over behavioral trajectories, feeding per-competency Bayesian Knowledge Tracing that estimates mastery within each domain; and (4) an expert judge agent synthesizes the domain-level estimates into an overall mastery score. Evaluated with 193 K-12 participants across 264 game sessions, the Agentic BKT pipeline yields mastery estimates significantly correlated with learning gain (r = 0.276, p = 0.0001) and post-test scores (r = 0.333, p < 0.0001) while showing no correlation with pre-test scores, providing both convergent and discriminant validity. The multi-agent approach approximately triples the predictive validity of a single-LLM baseline (r = 0.095, not significant) in this study, demonstrating that domain decomposition and session-level reasoning play a central role in capturing the multidimensional nature of financial literacy from gameplay

摘要：評估遊戲過程中的財務素養而不干擾學習體驗，仍然是教育性嚴肅遊戲中的一個主要挑戰。我們提出了 Agentic BKT 管道，一種多代理大型語言模型架構，用於從開放式遊戲事件中隱秘評估財務能力。該管道通過四個階段處理來自與 OECD/INFE 財務素養框架對齊的 2D 平台遊戲的事件：(1) 遊戲將每個玩家的決策捕捉為結構化事件日誌；(2) LLM 事件分類器根據三位領域專家的驗證標記每個行動，使用四點評分標準（Fleiss kappa = 0.624，實質性一致）；(3) 四個專注於風險緩解、投資、消費和信用管理的領域特定代理在行為軌跡上進行會話級推理，提供每個能力的貝葉斯知識追蹤，估計每個領域的掌握情況；(4) 一個專家評判代理將領域級估計綜合成整體掌握分數。在 193 名 K-12 參與者和 264 次遊戲會話的評估中，Agentic BKT 管道產生的掌握估計與學習增益顯著相關（r = 0.276，p = 0.0001）以及後測分數（r = 0.333，p < 0.0001），而與前測分數無相關性，提供了收斂和區別的有效性。這種多代理方法在本研究中將單一 LLM 基準的預測有效性大約提高了三倍（r = 0.095，不顯著），顯示出領域分解和會話級推理在捕捉遊戲中財務素養的多維性方面發揮了核心作用。

##### **Hybrid-IR: Dual-Path Hybrid Retrieval with Iterative Reasoning for Complex Medical Question Answering**
2606.25338v1 by Sheng Wan, Jiahui Zhang, Zicheng Zhao, Shougang Ren

Large language models (LLMs) have shown promising performance across a wide range of biomedical applications, including medical question answering (QA), yet they remain prone to hallucinations and outdated knowledge. Although retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) can alleviate this issue by incorporating external documents, there still exist two fundamental limitations. First, medical knowledge is often fragmented across documents, while most RAG methods rely on a single retrieval path, which makes it challenging to jointly preserve fine-grained semantic information and structured global associations. Second, static retrieval strategies are typically insufficient to support deep reasoning that is important in complex medical QA. In this paper, we present a dual-path retrieval framework with an iterative retrieval-reasoning mechanism termed "Hybrid-IR" for complex medical QA. The proposed Hybrid-IR integrates graph-based retrieval for exploration of structured knowledge and dense retrieval for fine-grained semantic matching. Moreover, the reasoning trajectory can be progressively refined through an iterative retrieve-reason loop. Experiments on three widely used medical QA benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of our Hybrid-IR.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在廣泛的生物醫學應用中顯示出良好的表現，包括醫療問題回答（QA），但它們仍然容易出現幻覺和過時的知識。<lb/>儘管檢索增強生成（RAG）可以通過整合外部文檔來緩解這一問題，但仍然存在兩個基本限制。<lb/>首先，醫療知識通常分散在不同的文檔中，而大多數RAG方法依賴於單一的檢索路徑，這使得共同保留細粒度的語義信息和結構化的全局關聯變得具有挑戰性。<lb/>其次，靜態檢索策略通常不足以支持在複雜醫療QA中重要的深度推理。<lb/>在本文中，我們提出了一種雙路徑檢索框架，並引入了一種稱為“Hybrid-IR”的迭代檢索-推理機制，用於複雜的醫療QA。<lb/>所提出的Hybrid-IR整合了基於圖的檢索以探索結構化知識，以及密集檢索以進行細粒度的語義匹配。<lb/>此外，推理過程可以通過迭代的檢索-推理循環逐步完善。<lb/>在三個廣泛使用的醫療QA基準上進行的實驗證明了我們的Hybrid-IR的有效性。

##### **Decoupling Reconnaissance and Exploitation: Measuring the Capability Boundaries of LLM-Based Web Penetration Testing**
2606.25332v1 by Liwei Yu, Shuo Li, Ming Zhou, Ge Chu, Yan Guo

Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown promise for automated penetration testing, yet existing end-to-end black-box evaluations are highly susceptible to error cascading: failures in early reconnaissance can mask an agent's actual ability to exploit vulnerabilities. To more accurately characterize these capabilities, we propose a two-stage decoupled evaluation framework that separates exploit execution from reconnaissance. Using ground-truth injection and knowledge-driven ablation across 70 high-fidelity web vulnerability testbeds, our framework isolates exploitation performance from reconnaissance noise. We empirically evaluate five open-source penetration-testing agents, covering multiagent, monolithic, and graph-driven architectures, on a strictly aligned subset of 50 representative vulnerabilities. The results reveal a substantial capability gap. With accurate vulnerability context, agents achieve a functional success rate of up to 90.0%, whereas autonomous reconnaissance, measured by targeted vulnerability recall, plateaus at approximately 50.0%, primarily due to failures in parsing unstructured telemetry. Cross-architectural analysis further reveals distinct capability niches: multi-agent isolation is more effective for long-sequence interactions such as de-serialization, while monolithic and graph-driven designs perform better on short-chain injections and cross-session access-control vulnerabilities, respectively. This decoupled evaluation work provides a fine-grained benchmarking protocol and an empirical basis for designing next-generation automated offensive security agents.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在自動化滲透測試方面顯示出潛力，然而現有的端到端黑箱評估容易受到錯誤傳遞的影響：早期偵查中的失敗可能掩蓋代理實際利用漏洞的能力。為了更準確地描述這些能力，我們提出了一個兩階段的解耦評估框架，將利用執行與偵查分開。通過在70個高保真網路漏洞測試平台上進行真實數據注入和知識驅動的消融，我們的框架將利用性能與偵查噪音隔離。我們對五個開源滲透測試代理進行了實證評估，涵蓋了多代理、單體和圖驅動架構，並在一個嚴格對齊的50個代表性漏洞子集上進行測試。結果顯示出顯著的能力差距。在準確的漏洞背景下，代理的功能成功率高達90.0%，而自主偵查的效果，根據目標漏洞的召回率測量，則平穩在約50.0%，主要是因為解析非結構化遙測數據的失敗。跨架構分析進一步揭示了不同的能力利基：多代理隔離在長序列互動（如反序列化）中更為有效，而單體和圖驅動設計在短鏈注入和跨會話訪問控制漏洞上表現更佳。這項解耦評估工作提供了精細的基準協議和設計下一代自動化攻擊安全代理的實證基礎。

##### **Physics Question Scene Graph: Fine-grained Evaluation of Physical Plausibility in Text-to-Video Generation**
2606.25306v1 by Atin Pothiraj, Jaemin Cho, Yue Zhang, Elias Stengel-Eskin, Mohit Bansal

Video generation models are increasingly capable of producing realistic videos, but they still struggle to generate videos that follow basic physical laws. Compounding this is a lack of reliable granular evaluation methods for localizing and specifying physical law violations in videos. We address this by introducing Physics Question Scene Graph (PQSG), a hierarchical question-based evaluation pipeline. PQSG evaluates generated videos by checking their faithfulness to a prompt across objects, actions, and adherence to physical laws using a graph-based hierarchy of questions generated by a vision-language model (VLM), guided by high-quality in-context examples. By representing questions as a graph, PQSG introduces logical dependencies within questions, ensuring that each query is contextually valid. Moreover, PQSG provides granular assessments of which qualities of the video violate physical plausibility constraints. We validate PQSG by creating FinePhyEval, a dataset with physics-based prompts and corresponding generated videos from diverse state-of-the-art video generation models (Sora 2, Veo 3, and Wan 2.1), with each video annotated across multiple categories by humans. Using FinePhyEval, we measure the correlation between PQSG's fine-grained scores and human judgments, showing higher overall correlations than prior work. We also find that PQSG ranks closed-source models higher than Wan 2.1 on physical realism. Lastly, we show that the annotations we provide in FinePhyEval can also be used for subtask evaluation: we benchmark two strong VLMs on generating and answering questions, finding that while models can create human-like questions, they still fall short of human performance in answering them.

摘要：視頻生成模型越來越能夠生成逼真的視頻，但它們仍然難以生成遵循基本物理法則的視頻。更糟糕的是，缺乏可靠的細粒度評估方法來定位和具體說明視頻中的物理法則違反情況。我們通過引入物理問題場景圖（PQSG）來解決這個問題，這是一個基於問題的分層評估管道。PQSG 通過檢查生成視頻在物體、動作和遵循物理法則方面對提示的忠實度來評估生成的視頻，使用由視覺-語言模型（VLM）生成的基於圖的問題層次結構，並由高質量的上下文示例指導。通過將問題表示為圖，PQSG 在問題內引入邏輯依賴性，確保每個查詢在上下文中都是有效的。此外，PQSG 提供了對視頻中哪些特質違反物理合理性約束的細粒度評估。我們通過創建 FinePhyEval 來驗證 PQSG，這是一個包含基於物理的提示和來自各種最先進視頻生成模型（Sora 2、Veo 3 和 Wan 2.1）對應生成視頻的數據集，每個視頻都由人類在多個類別中進行註釋。使用 FinePhyEval，我們測量 PQSG 的細粒度分數與人類判斷之間的相關性，顯示出比先前工作更高的整體相關性。我們還發現 PQSG 在物理真實性方面將封閉源模型的排名高於 Wan 2.1。最後，我們展示了我們在 FinePhyEval 中提供的註釋也可以用於子任務評估：我們對兩個強大的 VLM 在生成和回答問題方面進行基準測試，發現儘管模型可以創建類似人類的問題，但在回答問題方面仍然不及人類表現。

##### **EPTS: Elastic Post-Training Sparsity for Efficient Large Language Model Compression**
2606.25285v1 by Ke Xu, Jiaqi Wan, Wenhao Hu, Han Pu, Xiaoyun Wang

Post-Training Sparsity (PTS) has emerged as a crucial paradigm for compressing Large Language Models to facilitate efficient deployment on resource-constrained devices. However, existing PTS methodologies are typically confined to Single-Sparsity optimization, necessitating a separate, time-consuming optimization session for each specific sparsity level. This rigid paradigm significantly hinders flexible deployment across diverse hardware scenarios, as adapting to a new sparsity requirement mandates a complete re-optimization process. To address these limitations, we propose Elastic Post-Training Sparsity (EPTS), a unified Multi-Sparsity framework that produces a single elastic model capable of maintaining robust performance across diverse sparsity configurations through a one-shot optimization process. Specifically, we design a Multi-Sparsity Hierarchy LoRA (MS-HiLoRA) mechanism that facilitates knowledge inheritance from low- to high-sparsity groups, effectively mitigating the competition for parameter reconstruction. Furthermore, we introduce a Multi-Sparsity Feature Mixer (MSFM), which significantly enhances the model's adaptability to pruning perturbations by dynamically fusing feature representations of varying sparsity granularities. Extensive experiments on LLaMA and OPT families demonstrate that EPTS achieves competitive performance compared to state-of-the-art methods like SparseGPT and Wanda, while offering significant efficiency gains by enabling multi-scenario deployment from a single optimization. our source code is available at https://github.com/xuke225/EPTS.

摘要：後訓練稀疏性（PTS）已成為壓縮大型語言模型的重要範式，以促進在資源受限設備上的高效部署。<lb/>然而，現有的PTS方法通常僅限於單一稀疏性優化，這需要為每個特定的稀疏性水平進行單獨且耗時的優化會話。<lb/>這一僵化的範式顯著阻礙了在多樣化硬體場景中的靈活部署，因為適應新的稀疏性需求需要完整的重新優化過程。<lb/>為了解決這些限制，我們提出了彈性後訓練稀疏性（EPTS），這是一個統一的多稀疏性框架，能夠通過一次優化過程生成一個單一的彈性模型，保持在多樣化稀疏配置下的穩健性能。<lb/>具體而言，我們設計了一個多稀疏性層次LoRA（MS-HiLoRA）機制，促進從低稀疏性到高稀疏性組的知識繼承，有效減輕了參數重建的競爭。<lb/>此外，我們引入了多稀疏性特徵混合器（MSFM），通過動態融合不同稀疏粒度的特徵表示，顯著增強了模型對修剪擾動的適應性。<lb/>在LLaMA和OPT系列上的廣泛實驗表明，EPTS在性能上與像SparseGPT和Wanda等最先進的方法具有競爭力，同時通過從單次優化實現多場景部署，提供了顯著的效率提升。<lb/>我們的源代碼可在 https://github.com/xuke225/EPTS 獲得。

#### Abstracts
##### **Towards Automating Scientific Review with Google's Paper Assistant Tool**
2606.28277v1 by Rajesh Jayaram, Drew Tyler, David Woodruff, Corinna Cortes, Yossi Matias, Vahab Mirrokni, Vincent Cohen-Addad

Artificial intelligence is driving a revolution in scientific discovery, accelerating everything from hypothesis generation to mathematical theorem proving. However, this rapid acceleration is creating a systemic challenge: traditional human peer review cannot scale to match the influx of AI-assisted science. Ultimately, to resolve this tension, we must also deploy AI to accelerate the verification and review process itself. To frame the discussion around this transition, we propose a taxonomy consisting of four progressive levels of AI-human collaboration in scientific evaluation, and discuss various trade-offs involved with each.
  As a step toward this future, we introduce the Paper Assistant Tool (PAT), an agentic AI framework built for deep scientific review and verification. PAT ingests full scientific manuscripts and produces a comprehensive evaluation, checking theoretical results, validating experiments, suggesting improvements, and identifying potential flaws. By utilizing inference scaling techniques, PAT is able to identify deeper issues than a single model call alone, achieving a 34% improvement over zero-shot recall on mathematical errors in the SPOT benchmark. Pilot deployments of PAT as a pre-submission tool for authors at two major Computer Science conferences -- STOC and ICML -- demonstrate its ability to identify critical errors and suggest substantive improvements to research papers. By catching errors early, PAT eases the cognitive burden placed on referees, while preserving their control over the outcomes of the review process.

摘要：人工智慧正在推動科學發現的革命，加速從假設生成到數學定理證明的所有過程。<lb/>然而，這種快速的加速正在造成一個系統性挑戰：傳統的人類同行評審無法擴展以匹配AI輔助科學的湧入。<lb/>最終，為了解決這種緊張局勢，我們還必須部署AI來加速驗證和評審過程本身。<lb/>為了框定這一過渡的討論，我們提出了一個由四個漸進級別的AI-人類合作在科學評估中的分類法，並討論了每個級別所涉及的各種權衡。<lb/>作為邁向這一未來的一步，我們介紹了論文助手工具（PAT），這是一個為深度科學評審和驗證而建立的代理AI框架。<lb/>PAT 會吸收完整的科學手稿並產生全面的評估，檢查理論結果、驗證實驗、建議改進並識別潛在缺陷。<lb/>通過利用推理擴展技術，PAT 能夠識別比單一模型調用更深層次的問題，在SPOT基準中對數學錯誤的零樣本召回率提高了34%。<lb/>在兩個主要計算機科學會議——STOC和ICML——中，PAT作為作者的提交前工具的試點部署展示了其識別關鍵錯誤和建議實質性改進研究論文的能力。<lb/>通過及早捕捉錯誤，PAT 減輕了評審者所承受的認知負擔，同時保留了他們對評審過程結果的控制。

##### **Vision-Default, Prior-Override: Causal Mechanisms of Perception-Knowledge Conflict in Vision-Language Models**
2606.28273v1 by Niclas Lietzow, Danielle Bitterman, Carsten Eickhoff, William Rudman, Michal Golovanevsky

Vision-language models must reconcile visual evidence with memorized world knowledge when the two conflict. How they resolve this conflict shapes the reliability of multimodal systems, yet prior work characterizes it behaviorally without a component-level causal account. We combine activation patching across three granularities (residual stream, attention heads, and MLP sublayers) with model-component ablation studies and mechanistic analysis. Across three VLM families, we find that visual grounding emerges by default, whereas prior grounding depends on a small set of causally necessary attention heads (2.5-4.8%) concentrated in the second half of the network. These heads enable answers from stored world knowledge (e.g., "red" for a strawberry) despite conflicting visual input. Ablating them flips predictions from knowledge-grounded to visually grounded answers in 68-96% of cases under prior-knowledge prompts, but changes only 0.8-7.5% of visually grounded predictions, establishing an asymmetric causal structure. The identified heads decompose into routing heads, which modulate information flow, and writing heads, which directly project answer tokens into the residual stream. This structure is consistent across model families and scales, revealing a sparse causal circuit underlying perception-knowledge conflict in VLMs.

摘要：視覺語言模型必須在視覺證據與記憶中的世界知識發生衝突時進行調和。它們解決這一衝突的方式影響多模態系統的可靠性，但先前的研究僅從行為上對此進行了描述，缺乏組件層面的因果解釋。我們結合了三種粒度的激活補丁（殘差流、注意力頭和MLP子層）與模型組件的消融研究和機制分析。在三個VLM家族中，我們發現視覺基礎是默認出現的，而先前的基礎依賴於一小組因果必要的注意力頭（2.5-4.8%），這些注意力頭集中在網絡的後半部分。這些注意力頭使得儲存的世界知識（例如，對於草莓的「紅色」）能夠提供答案，儘管視覺輸入存在衝突。消融這些頭部會使得在先前知識提示下的預測從基於知識轉變為基於視覺的答案，這在68-96%的案例中發生，但僅改變0.8-7.5%的基於視覺的預測，建立了一種不對稱的因果結構。識別出的頭部可分解為路由頭，這些頭部調節信息流，以及寫入頭，這些頭部直接將答案標記投射到殘差流中。這一結構在模型家族和規模上是一致的，揭示了在VLM中感知-知識衝突的稀疏因果電路。

##### **Agent-Native Immune System: Architecture, Taxonomy, and Engineering**
2606.28270v1 by Bo Shen, Lifeng Chang, Tianyuan Wei, Yunpeng Li, Feng Shi, Yichen Han, Peijie Gao, Shiyi Kuang, Xin Chang, Dehui Li

The transition from static chat bots to autonomous agents--equipped with persistent memory, tool-use protocols, and multi-agent collaboration--has fundamentally expanded the AI threat landscape. Current defense mechanisms, such as perimeter security and training-time alignment, remain external to the agent's active reasoning loop. Consequently, they fall short: a fully aligned agent remains highly vulnerable to runtime hijacking via memory poisoning, tool-chain manipulation, or multi-agent protocol attacks. To address this critical gap, we introduce the Agent-Native Immune System (ANIS), the first biologically inspired, endogenous defense architecture embedded directly within the agent's cognitive loop. Our framework presents four primary contributions. First, we design a six-layer Immune Tower (L0-L5), distinctly incorporating Barrier Immunity (L1) as a non-cognitive, physical-and-logical isolation layer. Second, we establish a unified taxonomy of Agent Viruses and Agent Vaccines, formalizing the critical distinction between superficial non-parametric defenses and robust parametric vaccines. Third, we conceptualize the Harness Triad--Meta, Self, and Auto--a self-monitoring, meta-cognitive automation backbone that drives Continual Immune Learning (CIL), enabling vaccines to dynamically adapt to novel threats. Finally, we establish a rigorous theoretical demarcation between model alignment and agent immunity: while alignment provides a static "constitutional" value foundation during training, ANIS serves as the dynamic "law enforcement" mechanism during runtime. We conclude by framing open challenges for the field, including immune protocol standardization, novel evaluation metrics such as the Autoimmunity Rate (false-positive intervention rate), and the co-evolutionary dynamics between pathogens and vaccines within collective intelligence ecosystems.

摘要：靜態聊天機器人向自主代理的轉變——配備持久記憶、工具使用協議和多代理協作——根本上擴大了人工智慧的威脅範圍。當前的防禦機制，如周邊安全和訓練時的對齊，仍然是外部於代理的主動推理循環。因此，它們無法滿足需求：一個完全對齊的代理仍然高度容易受到運行時劫持，通過記憶中毒、工具鏈操控或多代理協議攻擊。為了解決這一關鍵缺口，我們引入了代理原生免疫系統（ANIS），這是第一個生物啟發的內源性防禦架構，直接嵌入代理的認知循環中。我們的框架提出了四個主要貢獻。首先，我們設計了一個六層免疫塔（L0-L5），明確地將屏障免疫（L1）納入作為一個非認知的物理和邏輯隔離層。其次，我們建立了一個統一的代理病毒和代理疫苗分類法，正式區分了表面非參數防禦和穩健的參數疫苗之間的關鍵區別。第三，我們概念化了控制三元組——元、自我和自動——一個自我監控的元認知自動化骨幹，推動持續免疫學習（CIL），使疫苗能夠動態適應新威脅。最後，我們建立了一個嚴謹的理論劃分，區分模型對齊和代理免疫：雖然對齊在訓練期間提供了一個靜態的「憲法」價值基礎，ANIS則在運行時作為動態的「執法」機制。我們通過框架化該領域的開放挑戰作為結論，包括免疫協議標準化、新的評估指標如自體免疫率（假陽性干預率），以及病原體與疫苗在集體智慧生態系統中的共同演化動態。

##### **Learning Topology-Aware Representations via Test-Time Adaptation for Anomaly Segmentation**
2606.28268v1 by Ali Zia, Usman Ali, Abdul Rehman, Umer Ramzan, Kang Han, Muhammad Faheem, Shahnawaz Qureshi, Wei Xiang

Test-time adaptation (TTA) has emerged as a promising paradigm for mitigating distribution shifts in deep models. However, existing TTA approaches for anomaly segmentation remain limited by their reliance on pixel-level heuristics, such as confidence thresholding or entropy minimisation, which fail to preserve structural consistency under noise and texture variation. Moreover, they typically treat anomaly maps as flat intensity fields, ignoring the higher-order spatial relationships that characterise complex defect geometries. We introduce TopoTTA (Topological Test-Time Adaptation), a novel framework that integrates persistent homology, a tool from topological data analysis, into the TTA pipeline to enforce geometric and structural coherence during adaptation. By applying multi-level cubical complex filtration to anomaly score maps, TopoTTA derives robust topological pseudo-labels that guide a lightweight test-time classifier, enhancing segmentation quality without retraining the backbone model. The approach avoids reliance on method-specific raw-score thresholding for mask binarisation, preserves connectivity, and generalises across both 2D and 3D modalities. Extensive experiments across six standard benchmarks (MVTec AD, VisA, Real-IAD, MVTec 3D-AD, AnomalyShapeNet, and MVTec LOCO) demonstrate an average 15% F1 improvement over state-of-the-art unsupervised anomaly detection and segmentation methods, with the largest gains on anomalies exhibiting complex geometric or structural variations. These findings suggest that integrating topological reasoning into test-time adaptation provides a principled route to structure-aware generalisation, bridging the gap between geometric learning and robust adaptation.

摘要：測試時適應（TTA）已成為減輕深度模型中分佈變化的有前景的範式。<lb/>然而，現有的針對異常分割的 TTA 方法仍然受到其依賴於像素級啟發式的限制，例如置信度閾值或熵最小化，這些方法未能在噪聲和紋理變化下保持結構一致性。<lb/>此外，它們通常將異常圖視為平坦的強度場，忽略了特徵複雜缺陷幾何形狀的高階空間關係。<lb/>我們提出了 TopoTTA（拓撲測試時適應），這是一個新穎的框架，將持久同調這一拓撲數據分析工具整合到 TTA 流程中，以在適應過程中強化幾何和結構一致性。<lb/>通過對異常分數圖應用多級立方複雜濾波，TopoTTA 生成穩健的拓撲偽標籤，指導輕量級的測試時分類器，在不重新訓練主幹模型的情況下提高分割質量。<lb/>該方法避免依賴於特定方法的原始分數閾值進行掩碼二值化，保持連通性，並在 2D 和 3D 模態中均具有良好的泛化能力。<lb/>在六個標準基準（MVTec AD、VisA、Real-IAD、MVTec 3D-AD、AnomalyShapeNet 和 MVTec LOCO）上進行的廣泛實驗顯示，相較於最先進的無監督異常檢測和分割方法，平均 F1 改進了 15%，在顯示複雜幾何或結構變化的異常上獲得了最大的增益。<lb/>這些發現表明，將拓撲推理整合到測試時適應中提供了一條有原則的結構感知泛化之路，橋接了幾何學習與穩健適應之間的鴻溝。

##### **HPRO: Hierarchical Progressive Reward Optimization via Preference Extraction for Emotional Text-to-Speech**
2606.28249v1 by Sihang Nie, Xiaofen Xing, Rui Xing, Haoming Li, Ruitong Xiao, Jingyuan Xing, Baiji Liu, Xiangmin Xu

Recently, Large Language Model (LLM)-based Text-to-Speech (TTS) models have achieved remarkable naturalness. However, the standard Supervised Fine-Tuning paradigm often converges to statistically averaged prosody, limiting emotional expressiveness. While preference-driven optimization offers a promising alternative, existing approaches suffer from two structural mismatches: information conflict, where content and emotion in a shared latent space produce conflicting gradients, leading to reward hacking and semantic degradation; and scale gap, where sparse sentence-level rewards struggle to guide dense frame-level generation. To overcome these challenges, we propose HPRO, a hierarchical progressive reward optimization framework. Within HPRO, we introduce the HD-Emo codec as a novel differentiable reward model to resolve the information conflict. It extracts speech into distinct content and style preference tokens, structurally isolating emotional optimization from semantic content. Building upon this structured preference space, HPRO bridges the scale gap by progressively aligning frame-, word- and sentence-level objectives. Experiments demonstrate that HPRO significantly enhances emotional expressiveness, while effectively preserving linguistic intelligibility. The code and audio samples are publicly available at https://xxh333.github.io/hpro-demo/.

摘要：最近，基於大型語言模型（LLM）的文本到語音（TTS）模型已達到顯著的自然度。<lb/>然而，標準的監督微調範式通常會收斂到統計平均的韻律，限制了情感的表達。<lb/>雖然基於偏好的優化提供了一個有希望的替代方案，但現有的方法存在兩個結構性不匹配：信息衝突，即在共享潛在空間中內容和情感產生衝突的梯度，導致獎勵黑客和語義退化；以及規模差距，即稀疏的句子級獎勵難以指導密集的幀級生成。<lb/>為了克服這些挑戰，我們提出了HPRO，一個分層漸進的獎勵優化框架。<lb/>在HPRO中，我們引入了HD-Emo編解碼器，作為一種新穎的可微分獎勵模型，以解決信息衝突。<lb/>它將語音提取為不同的內容和風格偏好標記，結構上將情感優化與語義內容隔離。<lb/>基於這一結構化的偏好空間，HPRO通過逐步對齊幀、詞和句子級目標來彌補規模差距。<lb/>實驗表明，HPRO顯著增強了情感表達，同時有效保持了語言的可理解性。<lb/>代碼和音頻樣本可在 https://xxh333.github.io/hpro-demo/ 上公開獲取。

##### **How Width and Data Shape Generalization Scaling Laws in Quadratic Neural Networks**
2606.28242v1 by Julius Girardin, Emanuele Troiani, Yizhou Xu, Vittorio Erba, Florent Krzakala, Lenka Zdeborová

Understanding how performance scales jointly with model size and data is a central problem in modern machine learning. Existing theoretical works on scaling laws typically describe generalization as a function of data or compute, often in fixed-feature or infinite-width regimes and for online SGD. Here, we instead study how generalization scales with the number of trainable parameters and the number of samples in a feature-learning model. We analyze $\ell_2$-regularized empirical test error minimization in a quadratic two-layer network in a finite-sample setting with structured data. This setting allows for an explicit characterization of the generalization error as a function of the number of samples, model width, and regularization. Our results reveal a phase diagram with distinct scaling regimes as the number of parameters varies. In particular, the generalization error follows data-dependent power laws controlled by the spectral structure of the target. We further characterize the transitions between regimes, including the onset of interpolation, and their impact on generalization.

摘要：理解性能如何與模型大小和數據共同擴展是現代機器學習中的一個核心問題。現有的關於擴展法則的理論工作通常將泛化描述為數據或計算的函數，通常在固定特徵或無限寬度的範疇內，並針對在線 SGD。在這裡，我們則研究在特徵學習模型中，泛化如何隨著可訓練參數的數量和樣本的數量而擴展。我們分析了在有限樣本設置下，結構化數據中二次兩層網絡的 $\ell_2$ 正則化實證測試誤差最小化。這一設置允許我們明確地描述泛化誤差作為樣本數量、模型寬度和正則化的函數。我的結果揭示了一個相圖，隨著參數數量的變化而出現不同的擴展範疇。特別是，泛化誤差遵循由目標的譜結構控制的數據依賴性冪法則。我們進一步描述了範疇之間的轉變，包括插值的開始及其對泛化的影響。

##### **Exposure Bias Can Alleviate Itself via Directional and Frequency Rectification in Flow Matching**
2606.28226v1 by Guanbo Huang, Jingjia Mao, Fanding Huang, Fengkai Liu, Xiangyang Luo, Yaoyuan Liang, Jiasheng Lu, Xiaoe Wang, Pei Liu, Ruiliu Fu, Ruqi Huang, Shao-Lun Huang

Flow Matching (FM) has achieved remarkable generative performance, yet it suffers from exposure bias due to discrepancies between training and inference. Existing mitigation strategies typically rely on static constraints or external heuristics. In this work, we propose that exposure bias itself inherently contains dynamic signals that can guide its own rectification. To leverage this, we introduce DEFAR (DirEctional-Frequency Adaptive Rectification). This framework simulates the single-step inference process during training to identify exposure bias. It utilizes directional and frequency-adaptive feedback signals from the bias itself to enhance the model's bias tolerance. It consists of two key components: (1) Anti-Drift Rectification (ADR). ADR treats inference-time drift as a signal to learn the direction to steer deviated states back toward the target. ADR endows the model with intrinsic active self-rectification capabilities; (2) Frequency Compensation (FC). Empirically, we observe that accumulated bias often stems from a lack of low-frequency components in high-noise stages, and exposure bias carries the missing frequency. FC leverages the bias itself as a self-feedback weighting factor to reinforce the missing frequency components. Experiments on CIFAR-10, CelebA-64, and ImageNet-256/512 show that DEFAR outperforms prior baselines and further demonstrates favorable scalability, compatibility, and inference robustness.

摘要：Flow Matching (FM) 已經實現了顯著的生成性能，但由於訓練和推理之間的差異，它遭受了曝光偏差的影響。<lb/>現有的緩解策略通常依賴於靜態約束或外部啟發式方法。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們提出曝光偏差本身固有地包含了可以指導其自身修正的動態信號。<lb/>為了利用這一點，我們引入了 DEFAR（方向頻率自適應修正）。<lb/>該框架在訓練期間模擬單步推理過程，以識別曝光偏差。<lb/>它利用來自偏差本身的方向性和頻率自適應反饋信號來增強模型的偏差容忍度。<lb/>它由兩個關鍵組件組成： (1) 反漂移修正（ADR）。<lb/>ADR 將推理時的漂移視為一種信號，以學習將偏離狀態引導回目標的方向。<lb/>ADR 賦予模型內在的主動自我修正能力； (2) 頻率補償（FC）。<lb/>根據實驗，我們觀察到累積偏差通常源於高噪聲階段缺乏低頻成分，而曝光偏差攜帶了缺失的頻率。<lb/>FC 利用偏差本身作為自我反饋加權因子，以強化缺失的頻率成分。<lb/>在 CIFAR-10、CelebA-64 和 ImageNet-256/512 上的實驗顯示，DEFAR 超越了先前的基準，並進一步展示了良好的可擴展性、兼容性和推理穩健性。

##### **Towards Value-Constrained Credit Assignment in Fully Delegated AI Cooperatives**
2606.28217v1 by Young Yoon, Jimin Kim, Soyeon Park

We propose a framework for reward allocation in fully delegated AI cooperatives where humans are represented by agents that contribute data and participate in model updates under heterogeneous value constraints. The key idea is to credit only those updates that remain admissible after screening them against each principal's value profile. We formulate value-conditioned gradient filtering, online marginal contribution signals, and cumulative revenue settlement within a traversal learning (TL) substrate. TL is especially attractive here because it performs decentralized backpropagation without the quality loss associated with aggregation-centric distributed learning and, we argue, offers a finer attribution substrate than FedAvg-style federated learning by preserving explicit traversal and gradient paths. The framework is positioned against data valuation, federated contribution estimation, personalized federated learning, and pluralistic alignment.

摘要：我們提出了一個框架，用於完全委託的人工智慧合作社中的獎勵分配，在這裡人類由貢獻數據並參與模型更新的代理表示，並在異質價值約束下運作。<lb/>關鍵思想是僅對那些在根據每位委託人的價值概況進行篩選後仍然可接受的更新進行信用。<lb/>我們制定了基於價值的梯度過濾、在線邊際貢獻信號和累積收益結算，這些都在遍歷學習（TL）基底中進行。<lb/>在這裡，TL 特別有吸引力，因為它執行去中心化的反向傳播，而不會因為以聚合為中心的分佈式學習而導致質量損失，並且我們認為，通過保留明確的遍歷和梯度路徑，它提供了比 FedAvg 風格的聯邦學習更精細的歸因基底。<lb/>該框架與數據估值、聯邦貢獻估計、個性化聯邦學習和多元對齊相對應。

##### **The Remittance Blueprint: Data-driven Intelligence for Sri Lanka**

This study analyzes Sri Lankan migration and remittances over 32 years (1994-2025). ##### **Cognitive Episodes in LLM Reasoning Traces Enable Interpretable Human Item Difficulty Prediction**
2606.28186v1 by Chenguang Wang, Ming Li, Xinyue Zeng, Zhuochun Li, Hong Jiao, Tianyi Zhou, Dawei Zhou

Predicting human item difficulty is central to educational assessment, where reliable estimates support fairness and effective test construction. Existing methods often depend on costly human calibration or item-level textual representations, providing limited evidence about the cognitive processes that make items difficult. We argue that difficulty should be viewed not only as a property of item text, but also as an observable consequence of the problem-solving burden an item induces. Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) offer scalable process evidence through reasoning traces, but such evidence must be structured to support interpretable modeling. To this end, we introduce Epi2Diff (Episode to Difficulty), a framework that maps LRM reasoning traces into cognitively grounded episode sequences. These episodes group trace segments into functional problem-solving states, enabling difficulty to be modeled through reasoning scale, effort allocation, and state transitions. Epi2Diff extracts compact episode-dynamic features and combines them with semantic item representations for human difficulty prediction. Experiments on four real-world human difficulty datasets show that Epi2Diff consistently outperforms strong baselines, including fine-tuned small language models, LLM in-context learning, and supervised LLM adaptation. On SAT-derived classification benchmarks, Epi2Diff achieves an 8.1% average relative gain over supervised LLM fine-tuning baselines. Further analyses show that harder items induce more effortful, iterative, and implementation-centered episode dynamics, rather than merely longer responses. These results demonstrate that cognitive episodes in LRM reasoning traces provide a predictive and interpretable process representation for human item difficulty, offering a new lens for educational measurement with reasoning models.

摘要：預測人類項目難度是教育評估的核心，可靠的估計支持公平和有效的測試構建。現有的方法通常依賴於昂貴的人為校準或項目級的文本表示，提供關於使項目變得困難的認知過程的有限證據。我們認為，難度不僅應被視為項目文本的一個屬性，還應被視為項目所引發的問題解決負擔的可觀察後果。大型推理模型（LRMs）通過推理痕跡提供可擴展的過程證據，但這些證據必須結構化以支持可解釋的建模。為此，我們介紹了Epi2Diff（從情節到難度），這是一個將LRM推理痕跡映射到認知基礎情節序列的框架。這些情節將痕跡片段分組為功能性問題解決狀態，使得難度可以通過推理規模、努力分配和狀態轉換來建模。Epi2Diff提取緊湊的情節動態特徵，並將其與語義項目表示結合，用於人類難度預測。在四個真實世界的人類難度數據集上的實驗顯示，Epi2Diff始終優於強基準，包括微調的小型語言模型、LLM的上下文學習和監督式LLM適應。在基於SAT的分類基準上，Epi2Diff相對於監督式LLM微調基準實現了8.1%的平均相對增益。進一步的分析顯示，更難的項目引發了更費力的、迭代的和以實施為中心的情節動態，而不僅僅是更長的回應。這些結果表明，LRM推理痕跡中的認知情節為人類項目難度提供了可預測和可解釋的過程表示，為使用推理模型的教育測量提供了一個新的視角。

##### **LLawCo: Learning Laws of Cooperation for Modeling Embodied Multi-Agent Behavior**
2606.28182v1 by Qinhong Zhou, Chuang Gan, Anoop Cherian

Embodied agents operating in decentralized and partially observable environments have attracted growing attention in recent years. To address this challenge, we propose a novel framework, Learning Laws of Cooperation (LLawCo), that enables embodied agents to autonomously align with both their partners and task objectives. Our framework allows agents to reflect on past failures to extract misaligned behavioral patterns, which are used to derive high-level behavioral laws, such as "Talk when necessary" and "Wait for partner." These laws are explicitly incorporated into the agents' chains of thought via supervised fine-tuning, aligning their reasoning with task requirements and the behavior of other agents. To evaluate our approach, we introduce PARTNR-Dialog, a large-scale multi-agent communicative and cooperative planning benchmark built on the PARTNR environment. Experiments on existing tasks and our new benchmark demonstrate significant improvements in cooperative efficiency and task success rates. Across four backbone LLMs, our method achieves average success rate improvements of 4.5% on the PARTNR-Dialog benchmark and 6.8% on the TDW-MAT benchmark over state-of-the-art open-source communicative agent frameworks. See the LLawCo project page for details: https://www.merl.com/research/highlights/LLawCo

##### **Tandem Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards**
2606.28166v1 by Difan Jiao, Raghav Singhal, Robert West, Ashton Anderson

Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has significantly improved the reasoning capability of large language models, reaching expert or even superhuman performance in domains such as competition math. However, whether weaker agents and humans can actually harness this capability is far less certain, with RLVR documented to drift reasoning toward idiosyncratic patterns such as poor readability and language mixing. Tandem training is a recently introduced paradigm that targets this compatibility problem: a trained, stronger senior co-generates each rollout with a frozen, weaker junior, and the two are rewarded as a team, so the senior is pushed to reason in ways the junior can follow. Yet this paradigm has so far been demonstrated only in proof-of-concept settings, leaving open whether it scales to the long chains of thought of the modern RLVR pipeline. In this work, we propose Tandem Reinforcement Learning (TRL), which carries the tandem training paradigm into RLVR. In TRL, the senior and a frozen junior alternate stochastically to co-generate the reasoning, the resulting generation is rewarded, and the standard GRPO loss is applied to the senior. Training Qwen3-4B-Instruct on competition math, we find that TRL matches vanilla GRPO on solo reasoning capability while three properties emerge together from the same rollout structure: stronger handoff robustness with the junior, reduced distributional drift from the junior, and a chain-of-thought more legible to the junior. Our results demonstrate a promising route for RLVR with practical payoffs in multi-model communication and human compatibility.

摘要：強化學習與可驗證獎勵（RLVR）顯著提升了大型語言模型的推理能力，在競賽數學等領域達到了專家甚至超人類的表現。<lb/>然而，較弱的代理和人類是否能夠實際利用這種能力則不太確定，RLVR被記錄到會使推理漂移向一些特異的模式，例如可讀性差和語言混合。<lb/>串聯訓練是一種最近引入的範式，旨在解決這個兼容性問題：一個訓練好的、較強的高級代理與一個凍結的、較弱的初級代理共同生成每次的推理，並且兩者作為一個團隊獲得獎勵，因此高級代理被推動以初級代理能夠理解的方式進行推理。<lb/>然而，這種範式迄今為止僅在概念驗證的環境中得到展示，尚不清楚它是否能擴展到現代RLVR流程中的長推理鏈。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們提出了串聯強化學習（TRL），將串聯訓練範式引入RLVR。<lb/>在TRL中，高級和凍結的初級代理隨機交替共同生成推理，生成的結果會獲得獎勵，並且標準的GRPO損失會應用於高級代理。<lb/>在競賽數學上訓練Qwen3-4B-Instruct時，我們發現TRL在單獨推理能力上與普通GRPO相匹配，同時從相同的推理結構中出現了三個特性：與初級代理的交接穩健性更強、來自初級代理的分佈漂移減少，以及對初級代理來說更易讀的推理鏈。<lb/>我們的結果展示了RLVR的一條有前景的路徑，並在多模型通信和人類兼容性方面具有實際的收益。

##### **Robust Harmful Features Under Jailbreak Attacks: Mechanistic Evidence from Attention Head Specialization in Large Language Models**
2606.28153v1 by Yanchen Yin, Dongqi Han, Linghui Li

Jailbreak attacks bypass LLM safety alignment, yet their mechanisms remain poorly understood. We provide evidence that attacks do not comprehensively eliminate safety features, but instead selectively suppress specific attention heads. We identify two functionally differentiated types: Adversarially Compromised Heads (ACHs) concentrated in early layers, which are suppressed under attacks, and Safety-Aligned Heads (SAHs) in mid-layers, which maintain robust activations even when attacks succeed. Ablation studies support the causal role of ACHs and the contribution of SAHs to robust activations: suppressing a small number of ACHs is sufficient to induce jailbreak-like behavior on normally refused inputs, while removing SAHs substantially weakens mid-layer safety activations. Token-level attribution further shows that ACH suppression is driven specifically by attack-template tokens, providing a mechanistic account of why attacks can bypass refusal decisions through ACH suppression while leaving internal safety signals sustained by SAHs -- a phenomenon we term Robust Harmful Features. To validate the practical significance of this robustness, we show that simply reading these persistent activations -- without any training -- yields competitive aggregate detection performance with strong adversarial robustness.

摘要：監獄破解攻擊繞過了大型語言模型的安全對齊，但其機制仍然不甚了解。<lb/>我們提供證據表明，攻擊並不會全面消除安全特徵，而是選擇性地抑制特定的注意力頭。<lb/>我們識別出兩種類型的功能性區分：集中在早期層的對抗性妥協頭（Adversarially Compromised Heads, ACHs），在攻擊下被抑制，以及位於中層的安全對齊頭（Safety-Aligned Heads, SAHs），即使在攻擊成功時也能保持穩健的激活。<lb/>消融研究支持ACHs的因果角色以及SAHs對穩健激活的貢獻：抑制少量的ACHs足以在通常被拒絕的輸入上引發類似監獄破解的行為，而移除SAHs則會顯著削弱中層的安全激活。<lb/>令牌級別的歸因進一步顯示，ACH抑制是特別由攻擊模板令牌驅動的，提供了一個機制性解釋，說明為什麼攻擊可以通過ACH抑制繞過拒絕決策，同時保持由SAHs支持的內部安全信號——這一現象我們稱之為穩健的有害特徵。<lb/>為了驗證這種穩健性的實際意義，我們展示了僅僅閱讀這些持久激活——不需要任何訓練——就能在強大的對抗穩健性下獲得具有競爭力的總體檢測性能。

##### **Toward Robust In-Context Segmentation via Concept Guidance**
2606.28149v1 by Zhigang Chen, Xiawu Zheng, Rongrong Ji

In-context segmentation (ICS) requires a model to segment target regions in a query image using only a few reference images and their corresponding masks, without updating any parameters. Despite recent progress, prior ICS studies have largely overlooked a critical aspect: system robustness, ie, whether the model can produce stable segmentation results for the same query under different references. In this work, we revisit ICS from the robustness perspective and introduce a novel paradigm, Concept-Guided In-Context Segmentation (CG-ICS), which performs segmentation by extracting high-level semantic concepts from references rather than relying solely on low-level visual matching. Specifically, CG-ICS introduces a concept reasoning module that uses an MLLM to propose candidates and a SAM3-driven scoring function with tree-search refinement to select reliable textual concepts, together with a parallel visual exemplar route that provides query-side spatial grounding via a simple context construction. Both the textual concept and the visual exemplar are then used to activate the segmentation capability of a frozen SAM3 backbone. Extensive experiments on standard ICS benchmarks demonstrate that CG-ICS not only achieves state-of-the-art accuracy but also substantially improves robustness, yielding a more reliable ICS system with significantly reduced variance across diverse reference choices.

摘要：在上下文分割（ICS）中，模型需要僅使用少量參考圖像及其相應的掩膜來分割查詢圖像中的目標區域，而無需更新任何參數。儘管最近取得了一些進展，但以往的ICS研究在很大程度上忽視了一個關鍵方面：系統穩健性，即模型是否能在不同參考下為相同查詢產生穩定的分割結果。在本研究中，我們從穩健性的角度重新審視ICS，並引入了一種新範式，即概念引導的上下文分割（CG-ICS），該方法通過從參考中提取高層次語義概念來進行分割，而不僅僅依賴低層次的視覺匹配。具體而言，CG-ICS引入了一個概念推理模塊，該模塊使用MLLM來提出候選項，並使用基於SAM3的評分函數和樹搜索優化來選擇可靠的文本概念，同時還有一條並行的視覺範例路徑，通過簡單的上下文構建為查詢側提供空間基礎。然後，文本概念和視覺範例一起用來激活凍結的SAM3主幹的分割能力。在標準ICS基準上的大量實驗表明，CG-ICS不僅達到了最先進的準確性，還顯著提高了穩健性，從而產生了一個更可靠的ICS系統，並在多樣的參考選擇中顯著減少了方差。

##### **Beyond Sparse Supervision: Diffusion-Guided Learning for Few-Shot Graph Fraud Detection**
2606.28134v1 by Liming Liu, Chao Hu, Mingfei Lu, Yiwei Ge, Xingle Li, Heyuan Shi

Graph-based fraud detection is essential for safeguarding large-scale transaction systems, where undetected anomalies may lead to substantial financial losses and security risks. Real-world fraud graphs pose two coupled challenges: sparse and imbalanced supervision, where verified fraudulent labels are scarce and heavily skewed toward benign accounts, and representation dilution, where spatial message passing may oversmooth camouflaged anomalies while spectral filters may suppress fraud-relevant mid- and high-frequency irregularities. To address these challenges, we propose ADC-GNN, short for Attention-guided Diffusion-Contrastive Graph Neural Network, a unified framework that combines diffusion-guided feature augmentation, contrastive representation learning, and multi-hop spectral attention for few-shot graph fraud detection. The diffusion component is formulated as a feature-space denoising augmentation mechanism rather than a full topology-generative graph diffusion model: it constructs noise-perturbed node-feature views under a cosine schedule and uses contrastive learning to stabilize node representations across perturbations. The spectral attention module further adaptively emphasizes fraud-relevant hop-level and relation-level cues. We evaluate ADC-GNN primarily on three public benchmarks and additionally report a proprietary real-world telecom transaction dataset with approximately 60,000 records as a private case study. Under the 1% training setting, ADC-GNN achieves consistent improvements over original graph fraud baselines and four protocol-consistent recent graph anomaly/fraud baselines on the public benchmarks. Additional analyses on split stability, training ratios, oversampling alternatives, module-level ablations, diffusion schedules, and runtime and memory-consumption comparisons further characterize the effective operating regime of ADC-GNN.

摘要：圖基於圖形的詐騙檢測對於保護大規模交易系統至關重要，因為未被檢測到的異常可能導致可觀的財務損失和安全風險。現實世界中的詐騙圖面臨兩個相互關聯的挑戰：稀疏和不平衡的監督，經過驗證的詐騙標籤稀少且嚴重偏向良性帳戶，以及表示稀釋，其中空間消息傳遞可能會過度平滑偽裝的異常，而頻譜濾波器可能會抑制與詐騙相關的中高頻不規則性。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了ADC-GNN，即注意力引導的擴散對比圖神經網絡，這是一個統一的框架，結合了擴散引導的特徵增強、對比表示學習和多跳頻譜注意力以進行少量樣本的圖形詐騙檢測。擴散組件被公式化為一種特徵空間去噪增強機制，而不是完整的拓撲生成圖擴散模型：它在餘弦時間表下構建噪聲擾動的節點特徵視圖，並使用對比學習來穩定節點表示。頻譜注意力模塊進一步自適應地強調與詐騙相關的跳級和關係級線索。我們主要在三個公共基準上評估ADC-GNN，並額外報告一個擁有約60,000條記錄的專有現實世界電信交易數據集作為私有案例研究。在1%的訓練設置下，ADC-GNN在公共基準上相較於原始圖形詐騙基線和四個協議一致的最新圖形異常/詐騙基線實現了一致的改進。對於分割穩定性、訓練比例、過採樣替代方案、模塊級消融、擴散時間表以及運行時間和內存消耗比較的額外分析進一步描述了ADC-GNN的有效操作範疇。

##### **PhysisForcing: Physics Reinforced World Simulator for Robotic Manipulation**
2606.28128v1 by Peiwen Zhang, Yufan Deng, Shangkun Sun, Juncheng Ma, Duomin Wang, Jonas Du, Zilin Pan, Ye Huang, Hao Liang, Songyan Huang, Ruihua Zhang, Enze Xie, Ming-Yu Liu, Daquan Zhou

Video generation models have emerged as a promising paradigm for embodied world simulation. However, both general-domain video generators and robot-specific data fine-tuned models can still produce physically implausible manipulations, including discontinuous motion trajectories and inconsistent robot-object interactions, which limits their reliability as world simulators. Through extensive experiments, we find that such physical instability mainly arises from two factors: deformation of moving objects and implausible spatio-temporal correlations among interacting entities, particularly during contact. Building on this observation, we propose PhysisForcing, a scalable training framework that strengthens physical consistency by focusing supervision on physics-informative regions through joint optimization of pixel-level and semantic-level features. The framework consists of a pixel-level trajectory alignment loss, which supervises DiT features using reference point trajectories, and a semantic-level relational alignment loss, which aligns DiT features with inter-region relations extracted from a frozen video understanding encoder. Extensive experiments on R-Bench, PAI-Bench, and EZS-Bench show that PhysisForcing consistently improves embodied video generation over strong baselines, improving the Wan2.2-I2V-A14B and Cosmos3-Nano base models on R-Bench by 22.3\% and 9.2\% (7.1\% and 3.7\% over vanilla finetuning), with the Cosmos3-Nano variant attaining the best overall score. Beyond generation, as a world model under the WorldArena action-planner protocol it raises the closed-loop success rate from 16.0\% to 24.0\% and further improves downstream policy success, indicating that physically aligned video models yield stronger representations for robotic manipulation.

摘要：視頻生成模型已成為具身世界模擬的一個有前景的範式。<lb/>然而，通用領域的視頻生成器和針對機器人特定數據進行微調的模型仍然可能產生物理上不合理的操作，包括不連續的運動軌跡和不一致的機器人-物體互動，這限制了它們作為世界模擬器的可靠性。<lb/>通過廣泛的實驗，我們發現這種物理不穩定性主要源於兩個因素：移動物體的變形和互動實體之間不合理的時空關聯，特別是在接觸期間。<lb/>基於這一觀察，我們提出了PhysisForcing，一個可擴展的訓練框架，通過對物理信息區域的集中監督來加強物理一致性，通過像素級和語義級特徵的聯合優化。<lb/>該框架由一個像素級軌跡對齊損失組成，該損失使用參考點軌跡來監督DiT特徵，以及一個語義級關係對齊損失，該損失將DiT特徵與從凍結的視頻理解編碼器中提取的區域間關係對齊。<lb/>在R-Bench、PAI-Bench和EZS-Bench上的廣泛實驗表明，PhysisForcing在強基線上始終改善具身視頻生成，將R-Bench上的Wan2.2-I2V-A14B和Cosmos3-Nano基礎模型的性能分別提高了22.3\%和9.2\%（相較於普通微調的7.1\%和3.7\%），其中Cosmos3-Nano變體獲得了最佳的整體得分。<lb/>除了生成，作為WorldArena行動規劃者協議下的世界模型，它將閉環成功率從16.0\%提高到24.0\%，並進一步改善下游策略的成功率，這表明物理對齊的視頻模型為機器人操作提供了更強的表示。

##### **From Tokens to States: LLMs as a Special Case of World Models and the Continuous Path Beyond**
2606.28127v1 by Paul Dubois

The AI community has framed the relationship between large language models (LLMs) and world models as a dichotomy: LLMs predict tokens; world models simulate reality. Yann LeCun argues in 2022 that reaching general intelligence requires abandoning autoregressive token prediction in favour of latent-space architectures. This framing is unnecessarily binary. Two claims will be defended. First, LLMs are a degenerate special case of world models: the state space is the set of all token sequences, the only action is appending one token, and world models are therefore a strict generalisation of LLMs, not a replacement. Second, there is a natural continuous spectrum from NTP to JEPA, with multi-token prediction, future-summary prediction, and next-latent prediction as intermediate stations already populated by current research. Moving along this spectrum relaxes the LLM constraints one by one. It also progressively surrenders the two practical advantages that make LLMs trainable at scale: internet-scale self-supervised data, and a transformer architecture co-designed for discrete token prediction. Both are examined as open research questions: the data question (the cliff from self-supervised text to instrumented action-labelled environments) and the architecture question (whether the transformer generalises to continuous-state prediction, or whether a new primitive is needed).

摘要：AI 社群將大型語言模型 (LLMs) 與世界模型之間的關係框架化為二元對立：LLMs 預測標記；世界模型模擬現實。Yann LeCun 在 2022 年主張，達到一般智能需要放棄自回歸標記預測，轉而採用潛在空間架構。這種框架不必要地是二元的。將捍衛兩個主張。首先，LLMs 是世界模型的一個退化特例：狀態空間是所有標記序列的集合，唯一的行動是附加一個標記，因此世界模型是 LLMs 的嚴格概括，而不是替代。其次，從 NTP 到 JEPA 存在一個自然的連續光譜，其中多標記預測、未來摘要預測和下一潛在預測作為當前研究已經填充的中間站。沿著這個光譜移動逐步放寬 LLM 的約束。它也逐步放棄了使 LLM 能夠大規模訓練的兩個實際優勢：互聯網規模的自我監督數據，以及為離散標記預測共同設計的Transformer架構。這兩者都被視為開放的研究問題：數據問題（從自我監督文本到儀器化行動標記環境的懸崖）和架構問題（Transformer是否能夠推廣到連續狀態預測，或是否需要新的原始）。

##### **Higher-Order Fourier Neural Operator: Explicit Mode Mixer for Nonlinear PDEs**
2606.28122v1 by Alex Colagrande, Paul Caillon, Eva Feillet, Alexandre Allauzen

Neural operators provide deep neural networks for learning mappings between function spaces. Among them, the Fourier Neural Operator (FNO) is particularly effective: its spectral convolution relies on low-dimensional Fourier-domain representations and can handle inputs at different resolutions. This design aligns well with settings where the Fourier basis diagonalizes the underlying operator, such as linear, constant-coefficient PDEs on periodic domains, in which Fourier modes evolve independently. However, nonlinear PDEs may benefit from an additional inductive bias, as they exhibit structured interactions between modes, governed by polynomial nonlinearities. To capture this inductive bias, we introduce the Higher-Order Spectral Convolution, a spectral mixer that extends FNO from diagonal modulation to explicit n-linear mode mixing, aligned with the dynamics of nonlinear PDEs. Our experiments on standard benchmarks show that the proposed Higher-Order FNO (HO-FNO) retains the efficiency of FNO-based architectures and consistently improves over other spectral neural operators. HO-FNO also performs on par with or better than state-of-the-art transformers and state-space models on several datasets, with stronger gains in highly nonlinear regimes, such as the Poisson equation with polynomial forcing, where a single HO-FNO layer outperforms FNO models with up to 16 layers. We open-source our code for reproducibility at: https://github.com/AlexColagrande/HO-FNO.

摘要：神經運算子提供深度神經網絡，用於學習函數空間之間的映射。在這些運算子中，傅立葉神經運算子（FNO）特別有效：其頻譜卷積依賴於低維的傅立葉域表示，並且能夠處理不同解析度的輸入。這種設計與傅立葉基底對底層運算子進行對角化的設置非常契合，例如在周期域上的線性常數係數偏微分方程（PDE），其中傅立葉模式獨立演變。然而，非線性偏微分方程可能受益於額外的歸納偏見，因為它們在模式之間表現出結構化的互動，這些互動由多項式非線性所支配。為了捕捉這種歸納偏見，我們引入了高階頻譜卷積，這是一種頻譜混合器，將FNO從對角調制擴展到明確的n-線性模式混合，與非線性偏微分方程的動態相一致。我們在標準基準上的實驗顯示，所提出的高階FNO（HO-FNO）保留了基於FNO架構的效率，並且在其他頻譜神經運算子上持續改進。HO-FNO在多個數據集上也與最先進的Transformer和狀態空間模型表現相當或更好，尤其在高度非線性範疇中，如具有多項式強迫的泊松方程，其中單個HO-FNO層的表現超過了最多16層的FNO模型。我們將代碼開源以便重現，網址為：https://github.com/AlexColagrande/HO-FNO。

##### **Mechanism-Driven Monitors for Preemptive Detection of LLM Training Instability**
2606.28116v1 by Ruixuan Huang, Yipei Wang, Wenyi Fang, Hantao Huang, Yifan Huang, Ansheng You, Zhenxing Zhang, Shuai Wang, Fan Wu, Yang Zheng

Frontier large language model training consumes massive accelerator fleets and long wall-clock computation, making stability failures costly when they occur. After a numerical or a hyperparameter fault has already destabilized the training dynamics, it may continue for thousands of steps while loss and gradient norms still appear normal. We study mechanism-driven detection of training instability by deriving internal monitors from the functional role of each critical module and from the earliest computational sites where failures are expected to produce measurable signatures. For low-precision flash attention, we monitor the spectral entropy of a QK bilinear decomposition, whose first-order term becomes abnormal before the loss fully collapses. For MoE routers, we derive indicators from their role in expert selection. Our fault-injection experiments on low-precision attention, large learning-rate, and combined faults show that these signals provide distinct signatures for different failures, triggering thousands of steps before loss divergence.

摘要：前沿的大型語言模型訓練消耗大量的加速器集群和長時間的計算，當穩定性故障發生時，成本非常高昂。在數值或超參數故障已經使訓練動態不穩定之後，它可能會持續數千步，而損失和梯度範數仍然看起來正常。我們通過從每個關鍵模塊的功能角色以及預期故障會產生可測量簽名的最早計算位置推導內部監控器，來研究驅動機制的訓練不穩定性檢測。對於低精度的閃存注意力，我們監控QK雙線性分解的譜熵，其一階項在損失完全崩潰之前變得異常。對於MoE路由器，我們從它們在專家選擇中的角色推導指標。我們在低精度注意力、大學習率和組合故障上的故障注入實驗顯示，這些信號為不同的故障提供了明確的簽名，並在損失發散之前觸發數千步。

##### **BiDeMem: Bidirectional Degradation Memory for Explainable Image Restoration**
2606.28112v1 by Xinrui Wu, Lichen Huang

Degradation-aware prompts, conditions, and latent priors are increasingly used in image restoration, yet they are usually judged by a single endpoint: whether the restored image obtains higher PSNR. This is a weak test of semantics. A condition can help by adding capacity, acting as a global correction bias, or exploiting dataset shortcuts, without becoming an interpretable degradation prior. We propose BiDeMem, a bidirectional degradation memory for explainable image restoration. A query built from restoration features and input statistics retrieves a compact top-k subset of memory slots. The same selected slot identity supports the restoration path at inference time and a training-only forward-degradation explanation path. The study centers on verifiability in a controlled multi-degradation NAFNet setting. New controls separate the gain from a correction head alone, a dense query prior, and a static global prior: these variants are 0.2588, 0.2586, and 0.2839 dB below BiRank, respectively. Strong residual supervision and a wider degradation head also remain below the full bidirectional memory model. Intervention probes show that BiRank preserves restoration quality while increasing wrong-prior and native-prior sensitivity, framing degradation memory as both a restoration module and a falsifiable explanation mechanism.

摘要：降解感知的提示、條件和潛在先驗在圖像修復中越來越常見，但通常僅以單一終點來評判：即修復後的圖像是否獲得更高的 PSNR。這是一個對語義的弱測試。條件可以通過增加容量、作為全局修正偏差或利用數據集捷徑來提供幫助，而不會成為可解釋的降解先驗。我們提出了 BiDeMem，一種用於可解釋圖像修復的雙向降解記憶。從修復特徵和輸入統計構建的查詢檢索出一個緊湊的 top-k 記憶槽子集。相同的選定槽身份在推理時支持修復路徑以及僅訓練的前向降解解釋路徑。該研究集中在可驗證性上，並在受控的多降解 NAFNet 設置中進行。新的控制將來自僅修正頭的增益、密集查詢先驗和靜態全局先驗分開：這些變體分別低於 BiRank 0.2588、0.2586 和 0.2839 dB。強大的殘差監督和更寬的降解頭也仍低於完整的雙向記憶模型。干預探針顯示，BiRank 在提高錯誤先驗和本地先驗敏感性的同時保持了修復質量，將降解記憶框架作為修復模塊和可證偽的解釋機制。

##### **Scaling limit of the Random Language Model**
2606.28105v1 by Eric De Giuli

We develop a quantitative theory of the Random Language Model (RLM), an ensemble of stochastic context-free grammars, in a scaling limit where the number of hidden symbols $N \to \infty$ while the grammar temperature $\tildeε_d \to 0$ at fixed $x = {\tildeε}_d \log N$. In this limit, the model admits a controlled description based on a large-deviation principle over rule-usage patterns. A semi-annealed approximation maps the problem to a class of Random Energy Models with nontrivial combinatorics.
  We show that the RLM exhibits a condensation transition at a critical value $x_c=1/8$, below which rule usage concentrates and language statistics acquire a nontrivial dependence on corpus length. A second characteristic scale at $x=1/2$ marks the onset of entropy reduction from its maximal value. Across these regimes, we derive explicit scaling laws for the number of distinct rules, entropy, and related observables, identifying distinct scaling, saturation, and critical regimes controlled by the interplay of grammar size, corpus length, and temperature.
  The theory resolves previous ambiguities regarding the existence of a thermodynamic transition and explains the slow approach to the large-$N$ limit as a consequence of the dependence on $\log N$. It further provides a unified framework in which universal statistical properties of language emerge from typical realizations of generative grammars, with implications for both natural language statistics and the behavior of large language models.

摘要：我們發展了一個隨機語言模型（RLM）的定量理論，這是一組隨機上下文無關文法，在一個縮放極限中，隱藏符號的數量 $N \to \infty$，同時文法溫度 $\tildeε_d \to 0$，在固定的 $x = {\tildeε}_d \log N$ 下。在這個極限中，該模型允許基於規則使用模式的大偏差原則進行控制描述。一個半退火近似將問題映射到一類具有非平凡組合學的隨機能量模型中。<lb/>
我們顯示 RLM 在臨界值 $x_c=1/8$ 處展現了凝聚相變，低於此值時規則使用集中，語言統計對語料庫長度產生非平凡依賴。第二個特徵尺度在 $x=1/2$ 標誌著熵從其最大值開始減少。在這些範疇中，我們推導出明確的縮放法則，涉及不同的規則數量、熵及相關可觀察量，識別出由文法大小、語料庫長度和溫度的相互作用控制的不同縮放、飽和和臨界範疇。<lb/>
該理論解決了先前關於熱力學相變存在的模糊性，並解釋了大 $N$ 極限的緩慢接近是由於對 $\log N$ 的依賴。它進一步提供了一個統一框架，在這個框架中，語言的普遍統計特性從生成文法的典型實現中出現，對自然語言統計和大型語言模型的行為都有影響。

##### **OSOR: One-Step Diffusion Inpainting for Effect-Aware Object Removal**
2606.28094v1 by Qinming Zhou, Chenxi Sun, Deyang Kong, Junhao He, Xiangheng Tang, Peike Yu, Haotian Wu, Leilei Cao, Linfeng Zhang

Real-world object removal is challenging due to two key difficulties: the target object's non-local effects, such as shadows and reflections, which are difficult to model, and the fact that user-provided masks are often inaccurate or incomplete. With billions of parameters and tens of denoising steps, diffusion-based models achieve strong removal performance at the expense of substantial computational cost, limiting their use in interactive applications and on edge devices. To address these challenges, we present OSOR (One-Step Object Removal), which simultaneously achieves efficient, effect-aware, and mask-robust object removal. Concretely, OSOR introduces: (1) an occupancy-guided discriminator for precise boundary supervision, enabling stable single-step diffusion training; (2) an alpha head that leverages knowledge from pretrained diffusion models to predict appropriate removal regions with minimal overhead, thereby handling imperfect masks; and (3) a semantic-anchored verification pipeline (SAVP) that filters noisy instruction-based triplets to produce effect-aware supervision at scale. Using SAVP, we curate CORNE, which contains 280K verified removal pairs, and further annotate AnimeEraseBench and TextEraseBench to evaluate performance on more complex removal tasks. Experiments show that OSOR surpasses strong multi-step diffusion baselines in perceptual quality while achieving $4\times$ to $30\times$ faster inference.

摘要：現實世界中的物體移除面臨兩個主要挑戰：目標物體的非局部效應，例如陰影和反射，這些效應難以建模，以及用戶提供的遮罩通常不準確或不完整。基於擴散的模型擁有數十億的參數和數十個去噪步驟，在計算成本上取得強大的移除性能，這限制了它們在互動應用和邊緣設備上的使用。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了OSOR（單步物體移除），它同時實現了高效、考慮效果和對遮罩穩健的物體移除。具體來說，OSOR引入了：(1) 一個基於佔用的鑑別器，用於精確的邊界監督，使得穩定的單步擴散訓練成為可能；(2) 一個利用預訓練擴散模型知識的alpha頭，能以最小的開銷預測適當的移除區域，從而處理不完美的遮罩；以及(3) 一個語義錨定的驗證管道（SAVP），它過濾基於指令的噪聲三元組，以大規模產生考慮效果的監督。通過使用SAVP，我們策劃了CORNE，該數據集包含28萬個經過驗證的移除對，並進一步註釋了AnimeEraseBench和TextEraseBench，以評估在更複雜的移除任務上的性能。實驗顯示，OSOR在感知質量上超越了強大的多步擴散基線，同時實現了$4\times$到$30\times$的推理速度提升。

##### **STAG: Spatio-temporal Evolving Structural Representation of Action Units for Micro-expression Recognition**
2606.28083v1 by Nandani Sharma, Varun Sharma, Dinesh Singh

Micro-expression recognition is challenging due to subtle and short-lived facial muscle movements. Existing methods rely heavily on apex-onset frames, overlook fine-grained inter-frame dynamics, and separately model spatial and temporal information, limiting generalization across datasets. To address these challenges, we propose STAG, a dynamic ROI-AU-coupled spatial-temporal network that jointly models motion flow and adaptive facial connectivity. The framework extracts optical flow from discriminative frames using magnitude-based selection and temporal attention. A dual-branch architecture combines an enhanced graph attention network for structured spatial reasoning with a transformer encoder for temporal modeling. A bidirectional cross-attention module enables mutual refinement of spatial and temporal features, while AU-guided dynamic connectivity adapts facial region interactions according to muscle activation patterns. The transformer captures subtle temporal dynamics beyond apex-based approaches, improving semantic consistency and interpretability for explainable micro-expression recognition. The fused representation is optimized using focal loss and evaluated on CASME II, 4DME, DFME, NaME, SAMM, and SMIC-HS. Extensive experiments demonstrate improved robustness, generalization, interpretability, and computational efficiency, confirming the effectiveness of adaptive relational reasoning, AU-guided dynamic connectivity, and deep spatial-temporal feature fusion for accurate cross-dataset micro-expression recognition.

摘要：微表情識別因為面部肌肉運動的微妙和短暫而具有挑戰性。現有的方法過度依賴於頂點起始幀，忽視了細微的幀間動態，並且分開建模空間和時間信息，限制了跨數據集的泛化能力。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了STAG，一個動態ROI-AU耦合的空間-時間網絡，該網絡聯合建模運動流和自適應面部連接。該框架使用基於幅度的選擇和時間注意力從區分性幀中提取光流。一個雙分支架構結合了增強的圖注意力網絡以進行結構化的空間推理，並與Transformer編碼器進行時間建模。雙向交叉注意力模塊使空間和時間特徵的相互精煉成為可能，而AU引導的動態連接根據肌肉激活模式調整面部區域的交互。Transformer捕捉超越基於頂點的方法的微妙時間動態，改善了語義一致性和可解釋性，以實現可解釋的微表情識別。融合表示使用焦點損失進行優化，並在CASME II、4DME、DFME、NaME、SAMM和SMIC-HS上進行評估。廣泛的實驗證明了改進的魯棒性、泛化能力、可解釋性和計算效率，確認了自適應關係推理、AU引導的動態連接和深度空間-時間特徵融合在準確的跨數據集微表情識別中的有效性。

##### **Ontology-Guided Evidence Path Inference for Multi-hop Knowledge Graph Question Answering**
2606.28076v1 by Yongxue Shan, Meihan Wu, Cundi Fang, Jie Peng, Xiaodong Wang

Knowledge graph question answering (KGQA) aims to answer natural-language questions by reasoning over structured facts. Existing multi-hop KGQA methods mainly rely on topic-centered expansion, which faces two key challenges: the search space rapidly grows with noisy mixed-type paths, and retrieved paths may fail to satisfy the semantic constraints of complex questions. To address these challenges, we propose OPI, an ontology-guided evidence path inference framework for multi-hop KGQA. OPI introduces a relation-centric ontology graph to capture the head-tail type constraints of relations, providing a compact interface for answer-side constraints. Based on this ontology graph, OPI first introduces a bidirectional retrieval mechanism by mapping the predicted answer type to compatible final-hop relations and combining topic-side prefix expansion with answer-side final-hop matching, thereby suppressing noisy mixed-type expansion. OPI further adopts an iterative refinement strategy to reassess retrieved paths and candidate answers under the question context, filtering type-compatible but question-irrelevant evidence for more reliable answer prediction. Experiments on WebQSP, CWQ, and MetaQA show that OPI substantially reduces the search space, improves Hit@1/F1 by 4.6/5.0 points on WebQSP and 8.9/3.3 points on CWQ over the strongest prior results, and achieves near-saturated Hit@1 on MetaQA with the retrieval module alone.

摘要：知識圖譜問答（KGQA）旨在通過對結構化事實進行推理來回答自然語言問題。現有的多跳KGQA方法主要依賴於以主題為中心的擴展，但面臨兩個主要挑戰：搜索空間隨著噪聲混合類型路徑的增加而迅速增長，且檢索的路徑可能無法滿足複雜問題的語義約束。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了OPI，一種基於本體的證據路徑推理框架，用於多跳KGQA。OPI引入了一個以關係為中心的本體圖，以捕捉關係的首尾類型約束，為答案端約束提供了一個緊湊的介面。基於這個本體圖，OPI首先通過將預測的答案類型映射到兼容的最終跳躍關係，並將主題端前綴擴展與答案端最終跳躍匹配相結合，引入了一種雙向檢索機制，從而抑制了噪聲混合類型的擴展。OPI進一步採用迭代精煉策略，根據問題上下文重新評估檢索的路徑和候選答案，過濾出類型兼容但與問題無關的證據，以實現更可靠的答案預測。在WebQSP、CWQ和MetaQA上的實驗表明，OPI顯著減少了搜索空間，在WebQSP上將Hit@1/F1提高了4.6/5.0分，在CWQ上提高了8.9/3.3分，並在僅使用檢索模塊的情況下在MetaQA上達到了近乎飽和的Hit@1。
